<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id79881_a97209-a4 alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-layout-overlay kt-row-overlay-normal"></div><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="inner-column-1 wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_dacfa0-4d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-79881_3be977-9e"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-center"></div></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id79881_52376f-36 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="inner-column-1 wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_a3bd0a-91"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id79881_46a35e-5b alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="inner-column-1 wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_88b682-e6"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading79881_4e6dd5-01 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_4e6dd5-01"><mark true="true" class="kt-highlight">Solo Female Travelers:</mark> Don't Miss Out on the Adventure of Your Dreams.</h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading79881_a001ea-3a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_a001ea-3a">If you're anything like me, you just can't wait to get out there and see as much as you can. But one thing might be holding you back: a fear of going solo. I get it—I've been there too.</p>



<p class="">Whether it's your first time traveling solo or your tenth, it's normal to feel nervous. <strong>That's why I started The Unanchored Passenger—to equip you with the travel tips, inspiration, and support you need to feel confident in your solo travels abroad as a female.</strong></p>



<p class="">Whether you're looking to visit a bustling city or escape into nature, I've got you covered with destinations like the Camino de Santiago, Argentina, New Zealand, and more.</p>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_260906-c9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading79881_87ca25-36 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_87ca25-36">Download My Free Travel Planner for Solo Female Travelers</h3>



<p class="has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-238a65e6458b17f9bbd5cfc89ae58549" style="padding-top:0;padding-bottom:0">When traveling solo as a female, it's all the more important to stay organized. I've created this travel planning template to help you keep track of your itinerary, destination details, safety information, and more.</p>

<div class="inner-column-1 wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_f80560-da"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading79881_03a776-6c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_03a776-6c">Hey there! I'm Mikala.</h2>



<p class="">There’s always been something about international travel for me that’s filled my heart like nothing else. In 2022 my world fell apart following a <a title="" href="https://unanchoredpassenger.com/after-a-broken-engagement-i-found-healing-through-travel/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">broken engagement</a>, and I picked myself up again by chasing more travel experiences, including hiking the <a title="" href="https://unanchoredpassenger.com/camino-de-santiago/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Camino de Santiago</a> solo. Now I've been to 30 countries and have been solo traveling for 10 years.</p>



<p class="">If you’re here because your heart is calling you to new places and you're looking for tips and inspiration as a solo female traveler, then you’re in the right place.</p>

</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_c485f9-09"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

</div></div>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Your Camino Starts Now Training System</h3>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Imagine starting your Camino feeling ready to enjoy every step of your journey instead of wondering if your body can handle it. But how do you get there? Check out the <strong>Your Camino Starts Now Training System </strong>with a training guide, various training plans, and more to help you prepare.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link has-medium-font-size has-custom-font-size wp-element-button" href="https://unanchoredpassenger.thrivecart.com/your-camino-starts-now-training-system/?ref=website-homepage" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Start Training for Your Journey</a></div>
</div>
</div></div>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Capture Your Camino Journal</h3>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Do you feel stuck trying to figure out how to document your Camino memories in a way that will be meaningful and easy? Maybe you’ve looked into journaling apps, random notes, or something else but nothing feels organized or inspiring. I get it—that’s why I created <strong>Capture Your Camino Journal</strong>.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link has-medium-font-size has-custom-font-size wp-element-button" href="https://unanchoredpassenger.com/capture-your-camino-journal/">Start Capturing Your Camino</a></div>
</div>
